User accepted engine-bound limit. **Lessons** (locked permanent): (a) Thai docx fonts come from THE THEME (`script="Thai" typeface="..."`) not the rFonts tags вҖ” readers MUST parse theme1.xml; (b) MS proprietary fonts (Cordia/Browallia/Angsana) cannot be installed вҖ” canonical mitigation is metric-equivalent free Linux fonts via fontconfig alias (Loma/Garuda/Norasi); (c) LibreOffice render engine вү  Word render engine even with identical fonts вҖ” fundamental limit; (d) per-conversion font-detection logging is essential observability.
